\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
Versatile Analog to Digital Converter (V\+A\+DC) driver for X\+MC microcontroller family. 

The X\+MC microcontroller provides a series of analog input channels connected to a cluster of Analog/\+Digital Converters using the Successive Approximation Register (S\+AR) principle to convert analog input values (voltages) to discrete digital values.

Each converter of the A\+DC cluster can operate independent of the others, controlled by a dedicated set of registers and triggered by a dedicated group request source. The results of each channel can be stored in a dedicated channel-\/specific result register or in a group-\/specific result register.~\newline


The Versatile Analog to Digital Converter module (V\+A\+DC) of the X\+MC comprises a set of converter blocks that can be operated either independently or via a common request source that emulates a background converter. Each converter block is equipped with a dedicated input multiplexer and dedicated request sources, which together build separate groups.



The V\+A\+DC L\+LD is split into G\+L\+O\+B\+AL and G\+R\+O\+UP related A\+P\+Is.~\newline
 {\bfseries{G\+L\+O\+B\+AL\+: }}~\newline
 
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Global A\+P\+Is act on the entire A\+DC module. Configures global configuration registers 
\item Allows configuration of the background request source of the V\+A\+DC. 
\item The clock related configurations for the V\+A\+DC module are configured in the Global A\+P\+Is/ 
\item The Global A\+PI names are prefixed by the {\bfseries{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+V\+A\+D\+C\+\_\+\+G\+L\+O\+B\+A\+L\+\_\+}} and they accept \mbox{\hyperlink{group___v_a_d_c_ga8cc559b855e4da85ee2f48bcd98405cb}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+V\+A\+D\+C\+\_\+\+G\+L\+O\+B\+A\+L\+\_\+t}} as one of its arguments. 
\item Configures the background request source of the V\+A\+DC. The A\+P\+Is which act on the background related registers are prefixed by {\bfseries{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+V\+A\+D\+C\+\_\+\+G\+L\+O\+B\+A\+L\+\_\+\+Background}} 
\item Configures the sample and hold unit of the V\+A\+DC. The A\+P\+Is which act on the S\+HS related registers are prefixed by {\bfseries{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+V\+A\+D\+C\+\_\+\+G\+L\+O\+B\+A\+L\+\_\+\+S\+H\+S\+\_\+}} 
\end{DoxyItemize}~\newline


{\bfseries{G\+R\+O\+UP\+: }}~\newline
 
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Group A\+P\+Is act on a V\+A\+DC group. Configures the group configuration registers 
\item Configures the queue request source of the V\+A\+DC. The A\+P\+Is which act on the queue related registers are prefixed by {\bfseries{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+V\+A\+D\+C\+\_\+\+G\+R\+O\+U\+P\+\_\+\+Queue}} 
\item Configures the scan request source of the V\+A\+DC. The A\+P\+Is which act on the scan related registers are prefixed by {\bfseries{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+V\+A\+D\+C\+\_\+\+G\+R\+O\+U\+P\+\_\+\+Scan}} 
\item Configuration of the channels of each group are done by the A\+PI which have a prefix as {\bfseries{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+V\+A\+D\+C\+\_\+\+G\+R\+O\+U\+P\+\_\+\+Channel}}. 
\item The Group A\+PI names are prefixed by the {\bfseries{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+V\+A\+D\+C\+\_\+\+G\+R\+O\+U\+P\+\_\+}} and they accept \+::\+X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+V\+A\+D\+C\+\_\+\+G\+R\+O\+U\+P\+\_\+t as one of its arguments. 
\end{DoxyItemize}~\newline

\index{VADC@{VADC}!XMC\_VADC\_GATEMODE@{XMC\_VADC\_GATEMODE}}
\index{XMC\_VADC\_GATEMODE@{XMC\_VADC\_GATEMODE}!VADC@{VADC}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{XMC\_VADC\_GATEMODE}{XMC\_VADC\_GATEMODE}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily enum \mbox{\hyperlink{group___v_a_d_c_gaf6e1bd0a77d688aa01f925813a939dff}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+V\+A\+D\+C\+\_\+\+G\+A\+T\+E\+M\+O\+DE}}}

Defines the condition for gating the conversion requests. It can be used to set the E\+N\+GT field of A\+S\+M\+R/\+B\+S\+M\+R/\+Q\+MR register respectively for auto\+\_\+scan/background\+\_\+scan/queue request sources. Use \mbox{\hyperlink{group___v_a_d_c_ga7301a91a61ae924e06ce8af584abe939}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+V\+A\+D\+C\+\_\+\+G\+A\+T\+E\+M\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+t}} for this enumeration. \begin{DoxyEnumFields}{Enumerator}

Defines the edge sensitivity of the trigger signal which can assert a conversion. Use \mbox{\hyperlink{group___v_a_d_c_gae8fa52881a7e25eaff9d3db30243c302}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+V\+A\+D\+C\+\_\+\+T\+R\+I\+G\+G\+E\+R\+\_\+\+E\+D\+G\+E\+\_\+t}} for this enumeration. \begin{DoxyEnumFields}{Enumerator}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily enum \mbox{\hyperlink{group___v_a_d_c_gae06a6bd7c67b0299fcbefdc5c3de1ec8}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+V\+A\+D\+C\+\_\+\+T\+R\+I\+G\+G\+E\+R\+\_\+\+I\+N\+P\+U\+T\+\_\+\+S\+E\+L\+E\+CT}}}

Defines the external trigger input selection possibilities, to assert a conversion. Refer the V\+A\+DC interconnects section of the reference manual for details of peripherals which can be used. Also refer \mbox{\hyperlink{xmc__vadc__map_8h}{xmc\+\_\+vadc\+\_\+map.\+h}} file for detailed definitions of the peripherals which can take the control of these enumeration items. Use \mbox{\hyperlink{group___v_a_d_c_gab1a3533b1757bbeb36f98054bbceb84e}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+V\+A\+D\+C\+\_\+\+T\+R\+I\+G\+G\+E\+R\+\_\+\+I\+N\+P\+U\+T\+\_\+\+S\+E\+L\+E\+C\+T\+\_\+t}} for this enumeration. \begin{DoxyEnumFields}{Enumerator}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{XMC\_VADC\_GLOBAL\_BackgndAddMultipleChannels()}{XMC\_VADC\_GLOBAL\_BackgndAddMultipleChannels()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{cmsis__gcc_8h_aba87361bfad2ae52cfe2f40c1a1dbf9c}{\+\_\+\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+I\+C\+\_\+\+I\+N\+L\+I\+NE}} void X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+V\+A\+D\+C\+\_\+\+G\+L\+O\+B\+A\+L\+\_\+\+Backgnd\+Add\+Multiple\+Channels (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___v_a_d_c_ga8cc559b855e4da85ee2f48bcd98405cb}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+V\+A\+D\+C\+\_\+\+G\+L\+O\+B\+A\+L\+\_\+t}} $\ast$const}]{global\+\_\+ptr,  }\item[{const uint32\+\_\+t}]{grp\+\_\+num,  }\item[{const uint32\+\_\+t}]{ch\+\_\+mask }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em global\+\_\+ptr} & Pointer to the V\+A\+DC module \\
\hline
{\em grp\+\_\+num} & ID of the V\+A\+DC group whose unprioritized channels have been assigned to background scan \\
\hline
{\em ch\+\_\+mask} & Mask word indicating channels which form part of scan conversion sequence Bit location 0/1/2/3/4/5/6/7 represents channels-\/0/1/2/3/4/5/6/7 respectively. To Add the channel to the scan sequence enable the respective bit. Passing a 0x0 will clear all the previously selected channels ~\newline
Range\+: \mbox{[}0x0 to 0x\+FF\mbox{]} \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
None
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Description\+:}
Adds multiple channels to the scan sequence.~\newline
~\newline
Call this A\+PI to insert a multiple channels into the scan request source. This will be added to a scan sequence. The added channels will be a part of the conversion sequence when the next load event occurs. A call to this A\+PI would configure the register bit fields of B\+R\+S\+S\+EL.
\end{DoxyParagraph}

\end{DoxyParagraph}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{cmsis__gcc_8h_aba87361bfad2ae52cfe2f40c1a1dbf9c}{\+\_\+\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+I\+C\+\_\+\+I\+N\+L\+I\+NE}} void X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+V\+A\+D\+C\+\_\+\+G\+L\+O\+B\+A\+L\+\_\+\+Backgnd\+Remove\+Multiple\+Channels (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___v_a_d_c_ga8cc559b855e4da85ee2f48bcd98405cb}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+V\+A\+D\+C\+\_\+\+G\+L\+O\+B\+A\+L\+\_\+t}} $\ast$const}]{global\+\_\+ptr,  }\item[{const uint32\+\_\+t}]{grp\+\_\+num,  }\item[{const uint32\+\_\+t}]{ch\+\_\+mask }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em global\+\_\+ptr} & Pointer to the V\+A\+DC module \\
\hline
{\em grp\+\_\+num} & ID of the V\+A\+DC group whose unprioritized channels have been assigned to background scan \\
\hline
{\em ch\+\_\+mask} & Mask word indicating channels which form part of scan conversion sequence Bit location 0/1/2/3/4/5/6/7 represents channels-\/0/1/2/3/4/5/6/7 respectively. To Add the channel to the scan sequence enable the respective bit. Passing a 0x0 will clear all the previously selected channels ~\newline

\hline

\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Description\+:}
Removes multiple channels to the scan sequence.~\newline
~\newline
Call this A\+PI to insert a multiple channels into the scan request source. This will be added to a scan sequence. The added channels will be a part of the conversion sequence when the next load event occurs. A call to this A\+PI would configure the register bit fields of B\+R\+S\+S\+EL.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily void X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+V\+A\+D\+C\+\_\+\+G\+L\+O\+B\+A\+L\+\_\+\+Background\+Abort\+Sequence (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___v_a_d_c_ga8cc559b855e4da85ee2f48bcd98405cb}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+V\+A\+D\+C\+\_\+\+G\+L\+O\+B\+A\+L\+\_\+t}} $\ast$const}]{global\+\_\+ptr }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em global\+\_\+ptr} & Pointer to the V\+A\+DC module \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
None
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Description\+:}
Aborts an ongoing background scan conversion(sequence).~\newline
~\newline
An ongoing sequence can be aborted at any time. The scan unit picks the pending channels one by one from a pending register and requests for their conversion. This A\+PI essentially clears the channel pending register thus creating an illusion that there are no more channels left in the sequence. A call to this A\+PI would configure the registers B\+R\+S\+MR, B\+R\+S\+C\+T\+RL, Gx\+A\+R\+B\+P\+R(if group is available) to abort the current scan sequence.
\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Related A\+P\+Is\+:}
None. 
\end{DoxyParagraph}

Adds a channel to the background scan sequence.~\newline
~\newline
Call this A\+PI to insert a new single channel into the background scan request source. This will be added to the scan sequence. The added channel will be part of the conversion sequence when the next load event occurs. A call to this A\+PI would configure the register bit fields of B\+R\+S\+S\+EL.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{XMC\_VADC\_GLOBAL\_BackgroundDisableContinuousMode()}{XMC\_VADC\_GLOBAL\_BackgroundDisableContinuousMode()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{cmsis__gcc_8h_aba87361bfad2ae52cfe2f40c1a1dbf9c}{\+\_\+\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+I\+C\+\_\+\+I\+N\+L\+I\+NE}} void X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+V\+A\+D\+C\+\_\+\+G\+L\+O\+B\+A\+L\+\_\+\+Background\+Disable\+Continuous\+Mode (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___v_a_d_c_ga8cc559b855e4da85ee2f48bcd98405cb}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+V\+A\+D\+C\+\_\+\+G\+L\+O\+B\+A\+L\+\_\+t}} $\ast$const}]{global\+\_\+ptr }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em global\+\_\+ptr} & Pointer to the V\+A\+DC module \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
None
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Description\+:}
Disables continuous conversion mode.~\newline
~\newline
Typically for a Background request source to generate conversion request, either a hardware trigger or a software request is a pre-\/requisite. Using autoscan feature it is possible to start the conversion once and allow the sequence to repeat without any further triggers. Once all channels belonging to a Background request source have been converted, a request source completion event is generated. Generation of this event can restart the Background sequence. By invoking this A\+PI the Autoscan mode of operations is disabled. A call to this A\+PI would configure the register bit field B\+R\+S\+M\+R.\+S\+C\+AN.
\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Related A\+P\+Is\+:}
\mbox{\hyperlink{group___v_a_d_c_ga21a33313512a524d4d06e0ba81cd4a67}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+V\+A\+D\+C\+\_\+\+G\+L\+O\+B\+A\+L\+\_\+\+Background\+Enable\+Continuous\+Mode()}}~\newline
 
\end{DoxyParagraph}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{XMC\_VADC\_GLOBAL\_BackgroundEnableContinuousMode()}{XMC\_VADC\_GLOBAL\_BackgroundEnableContinuousMode()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{cmsis__gcc_8h_aba87361bfad2ae52cfe2f40c1a1dbf9c}{\+\_\+\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+I\+C\+\_\+\+I\+N\+L\+I\+NE}} void X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+V\+A\+D\+C\+\_\+\+G\+L\+O\+B\+A\+L\+\_\+\+Background\+Enable\+Continuous\+Mode (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___v_a_d_c_ga8cc559b855e4da85ee2f48bcd98405cb}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+V\+A\+D\+C\+\_\+\+G\+L\+O\+B\+A\+L\+\_\+t}} $\ast$const}]{global\+\_\+ptr }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
None
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Description\+:}
Enables continuous conversion mode.~\newline
~\newline
Typically for a Background request source to generate conversion request, either a hardware trigger or a software request is needed. Using autoscan (continuous conversion)feature it is possible to start the conversion once and allow the sequence to repeat without any further triggers. Once all channels belonging to a Background request source have been converted, a request source completion event is generated. Generation of this event can restart the Background configure sequence. Every request source event will cause a load event to occur. A call to this A\+PI would access the register bit field B\+R\+S\+M\+R.\+S\+C\+AN.
\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Related A\+P\+Is\+:}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{XMC\_VADC\_GLOBAL\_BackgroundGetNumChannelsPending()}{XMC\_VADC\_GLOBAL\_BackgroundGetNumChannelsPending()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily uint32\+\_\+t X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+V\+A\+D\+C\+\_\+\+G\+L\+O\+B\+A\+L\+\_\+\+Background\+Get\+Num\+Channels\+Pending (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___v_a_d_c_ga8cc559b855e4da85ee2f48bcd98405cb}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+V\+A\+D\+C\+\_\+\+G\+L\+O\+B\+A\+L\+\_\+t}} $\ast$const}]{global\+\_\+ptr }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
~\newline
 uint32\+\_\+t Returns the total channels pending for conversion. ~\newline
Range\+: \mbox{[}0x0 to (0x8$\ast$number of groups)\mbox{]}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Description\+:}
Returns the number of pending channels.~\newline
~\newline
This A\+PI will read the pending channels register and will return the number of channels that are awaiting conversion. When a load event occurs the scan sequence is pushed to a pending conversion register. From the pending register the channels are taken up by the converter. When the A\+PI is called it would return the total number of channels pending (B\+R\+S\+P\+ND\mbox{[}{\bfseries{grp\+\_\+num}}\mbox{]}).
\end{DoxyParagraph}

\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Description\+:}
Initializes the Background scan functional block.~\newline
~\newline
The B\+A\+C\+K\+G\+R\+O\+U\+ND S\+C\+AN request source functional block converts channels of all V\+A\+DC groups that have not been assigned as a priority channel (priority channels can be converted only by queue and scan). Background Scan request source converts the unprioritized channels. Unprioritized channels however can also be used with queue and scan. But a channel which is prioritized can not be used with background request source.

\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Description\+:}
Determine if the channel is pending.~\newline
~\newline
This A\+PI will check if the Channel in question is awaiting conversion in the current arbitration round. When a load event occurs the scan sequence is pushed to a pending conversion register. From the pending register the channels are taken up by the converter. This A\+PI would return true if the channel is found in the pending register (B\+R\+S\+P\+ND\mbox{[}{\bfseries{grp\+\_\+num}}\mbox{]}).
\end{DoxyParagraph}

Removes a channel to the background scan sequence.~\newline
~\newline
Call this A\+PI to insert a new single channel into the background scan request source. This will be added to the scan sequence. The added channel will be part of the conversion sequence when the next load event occurs. A call to this A\+PI would configure the register bit fields of B\+R\+S\+S\+EL.

\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Description\+:}
Select Gating signal for Background request source.~\newline
~\newline
Passage of the trigger input to the request source can be controlled via a gating signal. Any one of the 16 input lines can be chosen as a gating signal. Trigger signal can be given to the Background request source only when the gating signal\textquotesingle{}s active level is detected. Additionally the Gx\+B\+R\+S\+M\+R.\+E\+N\+GT has to be configured for the gating signal\textquotesingle{}s active level. A call to this A\+PI would configure the register bit field B\+R\+S\+C\+T\+R\+L.\+G\+T\+S\+EL.

Select Trigger signal for Background request source.~\newline
~\newline
A Background request source will raise conversion request only if there were either a request from application or occurrence of a hardware trigger. This A\+PI selects one of the 16 input lines as a trigger line. This is needed when a hardware trigger is needed for the conversion of the Background request source. Refer to the reference manual to determine the signal that needs to be connected. A call to this A\+PI would configure the register bit field B\+R\+S\+C\+T\+R\+L.\+X\+T\+S\+EL.

{\bfseries{Details of function}}~\newline
 Selects the gating mode of background request source.~\newline
~\newline
Passage of the trigger input to the request source can be controlled via a gating signal. This A\+PI determines how the gating signal behaves, either active low or active high. If gating signal needs to ignored X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+V\+A\+D\+C\+\_\+\+G\+A\+T\+E\+M\+O\+D\+E\+\_\+\+I\+G\+N\+O\+RE should be used as the {\itshape mode\+\_\+sel}. A call to this A\+PI would configure the register bit field B\+R\+S\+M\+R.\+E\+N\+GT.

\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Description\+:}
Generates conversion request (Software initiated conversion).~\newline
~\newline
A conversion request can be raised either upon detection of a hardware trigger, or by software. This A\+PI forces the scan unit to generate a conversion request to the analog converter. It is assumed that the background scan has already been filled up with entries. A call to this A\+PI would set the register bit field B\+R\+S\+M\+R.\+L\+D\+EV.
\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Related A\+P\+Is\+:}

Ignores the sleep mode request for the V\+A\+DC.~\newline
~\newline
With the sleep feature enabled, the module will respond to sleep requests by going into a low power mode. It resets the E\+D\+IS bit of C\+LC register for enabling the sleep mode.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{XMC\_VADC\_GLOBAL\_GetDetailedResult()}{XMC\_VADC\_GLOBAL\_GetDetailedResult()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{cmsis__gcc_8h_aba87361bfad2ae52cfe2f40c1a1dbf9c}{\+\_\+\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+T\+I\+C\+\_\+\+I\+N\+L\+I\+NE}} uint32\+\_\+t X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+V\+A\+D\+C\+\_\+\+G\+L\+O\+B\+A\+L\+\_\+\+Get\+Detailed\+Result (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___v_a_d_c_ga8cc559b855e4da85ee2f48bcd98405cb}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+V\+A\+D\+C\+\_\+\+G\+L\+O\+B\+A\+L\+\_\+t}} $\ast$const}]{global\+\_\+ptr }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em global\+\_\+ptr} & Constant pointer to the V\+A\+DC module.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
uint32\+\_\+t Complete global result register value G\+L\+O\+B\+R\+ES
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Description\+:}
Retrieves the complete result from the global result register associated with the {\itshape global\+\_\+ptr}.~\newline
~\newline
 This A\+PI audits the result register G\+L\+O\+B\+R\+ES for the validity of the data. If the validity is assured, data is first read the global result register, cached locally next and subsequently returned to the caller.
\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
You can cast the return to a varible of type X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+V\+A\+D\+C\+\_\+\+G\+L\+O\+B\+A\+L\+\_\+\+D\+E\+T\+A\+I\+L\+E\+D\+\_\+\+R\+E\+S\+U\+L\+T\+\_\+t to easily access the register bit fields
\end{DoxyNote}

 Range\mbox{[}0x0 -\/ 0X0\+F\+FF\mbox{]}

\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Description\+:}
Retrieves the conversion result from the global result register associated with the {\itshape global\+\_\+ptr}.~\newline
~\newline
 This is a lightweight version of \mbox{\hyperlink{group___v_a_d_c_gad2c400f302f493ee0e76da76ba6a4998}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+V\+A\+D\+C\+\_\+\+G\+L\+O\+B\+A\+L\+\_\+\+Get\+Detailed\+Result()}}. The behavior is exactly the same, just that it is only the 16 bit numeric result returned back to the application instead of the complete G\+L\+O\+B\+R\+ES register value.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{XMC\_VADC\_GLOBAL\_Init()}{XMC\_VADC\_GLOBAL\_Init()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+V\+A\+D\+C\+\_\+\+G\+L\+O\+B\+A\+L\+\_\+\+Init (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___v_a_d_c_ga8cc559b855e4da85ee2f48bcd98405cb}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+V\+A\+D\+C\+\_\+\+G\+L\+O\+B\+A\+L\+\_\+t}} $\ast$const}]{global\+\_\+ptr,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{group___v_a_d_c_gab29cc658e459b86028aee8366da96536}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+V\+A\+D\+C\+\_\+\+G\+L\+O\+B\+A\+L\+\_\+\+C\+O\+N\+F\+I\+G\+\_\+t}} $\ast$}]{config }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}

\hline
{\em config} & Pointer to initialization data structure\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
None
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Description\+:}
Initializes the V\+A\+DC global module with the associated configuration structure pointed by {\itshape config}.~\newline
~\newline
 It enables the global access to registers by configuring reset and clock un-\/gating for selected devices. It initializes global class, boundary , result resources by setting G\+L\+O\+B\+I\+C\+L\+A\+SS,G\+L\+O\+B\+B\+O\+U\+ND,G\+L\+O\+B\+R\+CR registers. It also configures the global analog and digital clock dividers by setting G\+L\+O\+B\+C\+FG register. Refer related A\+PI\textquotesingle{}s to change the configurations later in the program.
\end{DoxyParagraph}

\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Description\+:}
Set compare value in the global result register for fast compare mode.~\newline
~\newline
 The result of a conversion will directly be compared to the compare value entered as part of {\itshape compare\+\_\+val}. The prerequisite is that the channel associated with this global register must select an I\+C\+L\+A\+SS which has the conversion mode configured as fast compare mode. Call \mbox{\hyperlink{group___v_a_d_c_ga2e6a5c936529f8bf35c81f662e5a57c9}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+V\+A\+D\+C\+\_\+\+G\+L\+O\+B\+A\+L\+\_\+\+Get\+Compare\+Result()}} after this A\+PI to

{\footnotesize\ttfamily void X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+V\+A\+D\+C\+\_\+\+G\+L\+O\+B\+A\+L\+\_\+\+Startup\+Calibration (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___v_a_d_c_ga8cc559b855e4da85ee2f48bcd98405cb}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+V\+A\+D\+C\+\_\+\+G\+L\+O\+B\+A\+L\+\_\+t}} $\ast$const}]{global\+\_\+ptr }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
None
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Description\+:}
Enables the startup calibration feature of the V\+A\+DC module.~\newline
~\newline
 It configures the S\+U\+C\+AL bit of G\+L\+O\+B\+C\+FG register to enable the startup calibration feature. After turning it on, it loops until all active groups finish calibration. Call X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+V\+A\+D\+C\+\_\+\+G\+L\+O\+B\+A\+L\+\_\+\+Enable() and X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+V\+A\+D\+C\+\_\+\+G\+L\+O\+B\+A\+L\+\_\+\+Clock\+Init() before calling this A\+PI in sequence. Calling the A\+PI \mbox{\hyperlink{group___v_a_d_c_gab3cd418bbe9227c9e8a66e550b1d8e52}{X\+M\+C\+\_\+\+V\+A\+D\+C\+\_\+\+G\+L\+O\+B\+A\+L\+\_\+\+Disable\+Startup\+Calibration()}} can disable the calibration feature at runtime.
\end{DoxyParagraph}
\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Related A\+P\+Is\+:}
